# Finance Tracker — Claude Internal Reference

> **📐 Full system reconciliation lives in [`ARCHITECTURE.md`](./ARCHITECTURE.md)** — every
> money formula, sheet tab, localStorage key, the gas model, and the cross-screen
> "reconciliation hazards" (where the same word means different numbers). Read it before
> touching any financial calculation. Last full audit: 2026-06-02.

## Stack
- **Framework**: React 18 + Vite 8 + Tailwind CSS 4
- **Charts**: Recharts
- **Deploy**: `npm run deploy` → gh-pages branch → gamboiuwu.github.io/finance-prog
- **Router**: HashRouter (required for gh-pages static hosting)
- **No backend** — all data lives in the user's private Google Sheet

## Auth & Security
- Google OAuth2 popup → access token stored in `localStorage` (expires ~1 hr)
- PIN hashed via SubtleCrypto in `src/lib/pin.js`; idle timeout re-locks session
- All API calls: browser → Google Sheets API v4 directly (no proxy server)
- **Never commit** the spreadsheet ID to public files — it is in `src/config.js` which is gitignored-safe since no financial data is in the ID itself, but the sheet is private-only-accessible via OAuth

## Google Sheets Layout
*(Full column-level detail + which screen reads/writes each tab is in ARCHITECTURE.md §2.)*
| Sheet tab | Purpose |
|---|---|
| Monthly Summary | Income/spent/goal per month (rows = months, cols = metrics) |
| Monthly Expenses | Budget categories: Type, Account, Priority, Expense, Monthly Allowance ($), Actual Spend |
| Allocation Transactions | Every deposit/spend: Date, Type, Amount, Desc, Account, Done (bool) |
| Allocation Summary | label/balance pairs incl. **Gas** row (gas balance on hand) — read by Summary |
| Expense Summary | wide key/value layout (PI, CI, wage, mpg, $/gal, deposits) — read by Summary |
| Subscriptions | Subscription items: Name, Start Date, Cycle, Amount, Notes |
| Inquiries | Commission inquiries: Card Name, Contact, desc, Status, Price Agreed, Paid Amount… |
| Commission Prices | Pricing tiers: ID,Category,Variant,BasePrice,ExtraChar,Bg*,RushPct,CommercialPct,… |
| Business Products | Product cards: ID, Name, StartPrice, Formula (JSON blocks) |
| Business Transactions | Sales log: Date, Client, Product, Qty, Unit Price, Revenue, Margin%, Allocs(JSON), Order(JSON) |
| Business Account Spending | Owner draws + direct bucket spends: Date, Account, Amount, Vendor, Description |
| Business Expenses | Business spending log: Date, Vendor, Amount, Category, Product, Payment, Notes |
| Work Sessions | Time-clock log: Date, Start, Duration, Products, Total Units, Total Profit, $/hr, Notes |
| Plans | Savings/affordability goals (Dragon/Goals): ID,Name,Scope,Target,Saved,Per Month,… |

**Subsystems beyond the budget core** (see ARCHITECTURE.md §3 for formulas):
Business (`BusinessExpenses.jsx`, 6 tabs incl. time clock) · Commissions (`CommissionPrices` +
`Commissions`) · Time Clock (`TimeClockView`, `Work Sessions` sheet) · Dragon AI assistant
(`DragonBot` + `lib/dragon*`, user's own Anthropic key) · Goals (`Goals.jsx` + `Plans` sheet) ·
Orders/shipping (`lib/orders`, `lib/easypost`, EasyPost via CORS proxy).

**Google Client ID**: see `src/config.js`

## Key Files
```
src/
  App.jsx               — Auth gate (Google token → PIN → app)
  config.js             — Spreadsheet ID, sheet names, OAuth config
  lib/
    auth.js             — Google OAuth2 token storage/retrieval
    sheets.js           — readRange, appendRow, clearRow, batchUpdateCells, etc.
    pin.js              — PIN hash, verify, failed-attempt lockout
    gasPrice.js         — EIA gas price API fetch
  pages/
    Dashboard.jsx       — Home: income stats, subscriptions, bill calendar, charts (~2000 lines)
    BusinessExpenses.jsx — Product formula builder + Sales tab + COGS tracking (~1600 lines)
    Budget.jsx          — 4-tab: Budget / Categories / Entries / Trends (Goals pending)
    Transactions.jsx    — Transaction log
    Actions.jsx         — Allocation + Business transaction history with delete
    Summary.jsx         — Year summary
    CommissionPrices.jsx — Commission price calculator
    Commissions.jsx     — Commission tracker
    GasPrices.jsx       — Live gas price display
    MonthlyDetail.jsx   — Monthly report detail
    Login.jsx           — Google sign-in screen
  components/
    ProcessIncome.jsx   — Income allocation modal (priority-first or proportional, ~500 lines)
    PinGate.jsx         — PIN creation/verification screen
    Nav.jsx             — Bottom navigation bar
    LoadingSpinner.jsx  — Shared spinner
```

## BusinessExpenses.jsx — Key Concepts
- **Product formula**: array of blocks `{id, category, type ('fixed'|'percent'), value, customName?}`
- `computeFormula(startPrice, blocks)` — waterfall: each block takes from `remaining`
- `computeFormulaProportional(actualRevenue, basePrice, blocks)` — scales fixed amounts by revenue/basePrice ratio
- **Profit = 'Profit' + 'Revenue' allocation categories** — both are summed for the Profit tile and Process button
- `profitMarginPct(steps, startPrice)` — returns combined (Profit+Revenue)/startPrice %
- **Unified category model (the source of truth — see the big comment block at top of the file):**
  - `BUILT_IN_CATS` — all formula-block categories (incl. Profit/Revenue/Other)
  - `CAT_COLORS` + `catColor(name)` — ONE colour lookup for every tab (replaced the old `EXP_CAT_COLORS`)
  - `EXP_CATEGORIES = BUILT_IN_CATS minus Profit/Revenue` (profit isn't a spendable cost)
- **Per-category ledger** (shared by Accounts + Insights): `balance(C) = earned(C) − spent(C)` where
  `earned(C)` = Σ sales allocs[C], `spent(C)` = Σ `Business Account Spending`[Account=C] + Σ `Business Expenses`[Category=C].
  Profit/Revenue rows tagged "processed as personal income" are owner draws → excluded from P&L costs (`IS_OWNER_DRAW`).
- **Tabs** (`viewMode`): `products` (Cards/Compare sub-toggle via `productView`) · `sales` · `accounts` · `expenses` · `insights`
- Sales tab reads `Business Transactions!A:H`; col H is `allocs` JSON `{category: amount}`
- **Accounts 🏦 tab** — `AccountsView`; now reads all 3 sheets so an Expenses-tab spend reduces the matching bucket balance (the Accounts↔Expenses sync). Modal history merges direct spends + expense rows (📒 tag).
- **Expenses 📒 tab** — `ExpensesTab`; reads/writes `Business Expenses!A:G`
  - Reorder thresholds stored in `localStorage` as `biz_reorder_thresholds` (JSON keyed by product ID)
  - `ThresholdModal` — set COGS threshold per product · `ReorderQAModal` — guided Q&A + copy-to-clipboard
- **Insights 📈 tab** — `InsightsView`; 3 tools, all reconcile with the ledger above:
  1. **P&L statement** (period: month/year/all) — Revenue − COGS = Gross; − OpEx = Net; net margin %
  2. **Spending Trend** — last-6-month bar chart of actual cash-out + MoM delta
  3. **Top Vendors** — ranked vendor spend with share % (from both spending sheets)
  - `monthKey(v)` normalises serial/`YYYY-MM-DD`/`M/D/YYYY` dates to `YYYY-MM` so all sheets bucket together

## ProcessIncome.jsx — Key Concepts
- Reads `Allocation Transactions!A:F` to find already-deposited amounts this month
- `calcDeposits(expenses, income, mode, alreadyByType)` — returns per-category deposit amounts
- Two modes: `priority` (fill P1 → P2 → P3) and `proportional` (split by share of remaining need)
- Surplus: income beyond all goals distributed by user-configured weight buckets

## Dashboard.jsx — Key Concepts
- Loads on mount: Monthly Summary, Monthly Expenses, Report Links, Gas Price, Subscriptions
- Subscriptions stored in `Subscriptions!A:E`, cycle types: monthly/annual/weekly/biweekly
- Bill Calendar: shows 30-day window with subscription due-date dots
- Month Close: stores `closed_{month}_{year}` in localStorage (soft close only)
- Statement: `printStatement()` generates a printable HTML page via `window.open()`

## Budget.jsx — Key Concepts (updated 2026-06-02)
- 3 tabs rendered: **Budget** (priority-grouped edit view) | **Categories** | **Entries & Trends**
- **Categories** reads `Allocation Transactions!A:F` (UNFORMATTED_VALUE) for current month → sums by `Type` (col B) → maps against `Monthly Expenses` allowances → groups by `Expense` category (Essentials/Stability/Discretionary/Subscription). Savings items shown separately/collapsible.
- **Entries** = flat sorted list of raw allocation rows for current month
- **Trends** = 3-month comparison (current, last, 2 months ago). `allAllocTx` state holds ALL allocation rows (not just current month); `allocTx` is filtered to current month. Load fetches all rows once; both states populated from the same API call. `Sparkline` renders inline SVG bars (48×24px, 3 bars). `TrendsView` groups by expense category, shows delta arrows + sparklines per item.
- `parseSheetDate(val)` duplicated in ProcessIncome.jsx — consider extracting to `src/lib/dateUtils.js`
- Allocation Transactions column B ("Type") matches Monthly Expenses column "Type" (item name like "Rent", not the expense category)

### New Tasks 32–34 (from Report-Issue feedback, 2026-06-04) — awaiting Execute Y/N
- **Task 32 — Income Figure Consistency**: Multiple Report-Issue submissions (2026-05-30, 06-01, 06-03 ×several) say income shows wrong/inconsistent numbers across tabs (Dashboard `$2,408.93`/`$2,901.88` vs. actual ≈$750 for the month; Summary "PROCESSED INCOME $1676.39 — not income logged this month"; "Income is incorrect in this tab"). Root cause: Dashboard already treats current-month Allocation-Transaction totals as ground truth (Dashboard.jsx:782-788) to dodge stale Monthly-Summary sheet formulas, but Summary, Trends, and the 6-month chart still read the raw Monthly Summary cells, which carry last month's value into a fresh month. PLAN: (a) extract one shared helper `currentMonthIncome(allocRows, monthlySummaryRow)` into `src/lib/income.js` that mirrors Dashboard's ground-truth logic (alloc totals when current-month rows exist, else sheet); (b) use it in Summary (PI tile), Budget Trends, and any place reading `Total Processed Income` for the *current* month; (c) leave completed/past months reading the sheet (they're frozen). Q1: Should "income logged this month" count only positive deposit rows, or net (deposits − spends)? Q2: Is the canonical month-income definition "sum of Allocation Transactions income-type rows" or "Processed Income (PI) from Expense Summary"? Q3: should past months ever be back-corrected from allocations, or stay as the sheet snapshot? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 33 — Spending Calendar shows income as spending (bug)**: Feedback 2026-06-03T17:24 — the Dashboard "Spending Calendar" heatmap colors days by *earnings* not *spending* ("it's SHOWING income as expenses"). PLAN: in the heatmap day-bucket reducer, split signed amounts — spending = Σ negative rows (abs) → rose scale; income = Σ positive rows → teal dot; never color a day rose from an income row. Audit the same sign-handling everywhere a daily/category "spent" total is computed so the mistake isn't repeated. Q1: should transfers between own accounts be excluded from both? Q2: keep the calendar on Dashboard or move to Budget→Entries per Task 24's answer? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 34 — "Close Month" banner persists after close (bug)**: Feedback 2026-06-03T16:55 & 17:22 — "may is already closed" / "It keeps asking me to close out May…I clicked the button." The Dashboard close-month banner keys off `closed_{month}_{year}` localStorage but still renders after close. PLAN: gate the banner on the same `closed_{closeMonth}_{closeYear}` key that the Close action writes; verify the key name/casing matches exactly (`MONTHS[closeDate.getMonth()]` + year); add a fallback that also hides the banner once the new month has its own allocation rows. Q1: should "close" be device-local (localStorage) or persisted to the sheet so it syncs across devices? Q2: after closing, show a small "✓ May closed" confirmation chip instead of the banner? Execute? Y/N:

### New Tasks 35–37 (best-practice expansions proposed 2026-06-05) — awaiting Execute Y/N
- **Task 35 — Emergency Fund / Runway Tracker**: A standard personal-finance resilience metric the app doesn't show yet: *how many months could you survive on savings if income stopped?* PLAN: (a) **Monthly burn** = sum of P1 (essential) + P2 (stability) `Monthly Expenses` allowances (the bills you can't skip) — same set the Income Forecast (Task 16) already computes, so the two reconcile. (b) **Savings on hand** = sum of `Allocation Summary` balance rows whose label is a savings/cash bucket (or `Monthly Expenses` items with `Expense='Savings'` actuals) — reuse the balances Summary already reads. (c) **Runway = savings ÷ burn**, shown as a Dashboard card: "🛟 X.X months covered" with a 3-tier color (red <1mo, amber 1–3mo, teal ≥3mo) and a thin progress bar against a configurable target (default 3 months, the common floor; 6 months = fully funded). (d) Tap to expand: the burn breakdown and a "you're $X away from a 3-month cushion" line. Zero new sheet tab; new localStorage `_fin_ef_target` (int months, default 3 — no financial data). Q1: Which buckets count as "emergency savings" — all Savings-category items, or a specific named bucket (e.g. "Emergency")? Q2: Target floor of 3 months, or do you prefer 6? Q3: Dashboard card, or a panel inside Summary→Year? Q4: Should burn include P3/discretionary (worst-case) or only P1+P2 (true essentials)? Execute? Y/N: **Y (built 2026-06-05)**
  - ✅ COMPLETED + VERIFIED (2026-06-05) — `EmergencyFundCard` component in Dashboard.jsx (right after `ForecastCard`, before `export default`). Plan defaults used: savings = **all Savings-category items** (Q1), target floor **3 months** with a 1/3/6-month picker (Q2), **Dashboard card** placed right after the Income Forecast card and before the Spending Calendar (Q3), burn = **P1 + P2 only** (true essentials, Q4 — mirrors `ForecastCard`'s `recurringAllow` set so the two screens reconcile). **Burn** = Σ `Monthly Allowance ($)` for P1/P2 items where `Expense !== 'Savings'`. **Savings on hand** = Σ net all-time allocations into Savings-category buckets (signed `amount` summed per `Type` from `allAllocTx`, using the app's +deposit/−spend convention). **Runway = savings ÷ burn**; 3-tier color (rose <1mo, amber 1–3mo, teal ≥3mo); collapsed header shows the headline "X.X months covered" + progress bar toward target + "$X away from an N-month cushion"; expand reveals savings/burn tiles, the 1/3/6 target picker, the P1+P2 essential-burn breakdown, and per-bucket savings balances. Self-guards (`return null` when burn ≤ 0). New localStorage `_fin_ef_target` (int 1/3/6, default 3 — count only, no financial data). **Zero new API calls, no new sheet tab.** Build passes.
- **Task 36 — Recurring Bill Auto-Detection**: Cut manual subscription entry by surfacing recurring charges the app can already see. PLAN: scan `Allocation Transactions` (already loaded as `allAllocTx`) for repeating signatures — same `Type`/normalized `Description` appearing in ≥2 of the last 3 months at a similar amount (±10%) — then infer cycle from the gap between dates (≈30d monthly, ≈14d biweekly, ≈7d weekly, ≈365d annual). Show a dismissable "🔁 N possible recurring bills detected" card on the Subscriptions modal listing each candidate (name, typical amount, inferred cycle) with **"Add as subscription"** (writes one row to `Subscriptions!A:E` via existing `appendRow`) and **"Ignore"** (remembers the signature in `localStorage._fin_recurring_ignored` so it never re-suggests). Skips anything already in `Subscriptions`. No new sheet tab; new localStorage `_fin_recurring_ignored` (array of signature hashes — no amounts/financial data, just opaque keys). Q1: Detection window — last 3 months or last 6 for higher confidence? Q2: Amount tolerance — ±10% (plan) or stricter/looser? Q3: Match on Description text, Type (budget item), or both? Q4: Auto-add high-confidence matches, or always require your one-tap confirm? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 37 — Encrypted Data Backup & Restore**: All finances live in one Google Sheet; if it's lost/corrupted there's no local fallback. PLAN: a "💾 Backup" action (Settings/Dashboard footer) that reads every sheet tab via existing `readRange`, bundles them into one JSON snapshot `{version, exportedAt, sheets:{tabName: rows}}`, and downloads it client-side (same `Blob`+anchor pattern as IssueReporter's export) — **encrypted at rest** with the user's PIN via SubtleCrypto AES-GCM (key derived with PBKDF2 from the PIN, reusing `src/lib/pin.js` primitives) so the file is safe to store anywhere. "Restore preview" reads a backup file, decrypts with PIN, and shows a per-tab row-count diff vs. live (read-only preview first — **never auto-overwrites** the sheet without an explicit, typed confirm). Keep it export/restore-preview only in v1; one-click sheet rewrite is a follow-up. No new sheet tab; nothing financial ever touches GitHub (the encrypted file is local-only). Q1: Encrypt with PIN (plan) or also offer a plain-JSON option for power users? Q2: Backup all tabs, or a chosen subset (skip the large Business logs)? Q3: Should v1 include actual sheet-restore (write-back), or preview-only until you've tested it? Q4: Add an optional reminder to back up monthly (e.g. on month close)? Execute? Y/N:

### New Tasks 38–40 (best-practice expansions proposed 2026-06-05) — awaiting Execute Y/N
- **Task 38 — Sinking Funds for Irregular Expenses**: The budget handles monthly bills and (via Subscriptions) annual renewals, but not the *lumpy, non-recurring* costs that wreck a month when they land — car registration/repair, insurance premiums, holidays, gifts, medical. Best practice is a **sinking fund**: decide the total you'll need and by when, and set aside `total ÷ months-remaining` every month so the cash is there when the bill hits. PLAN: (a) reuse the existing **`Plans` sheet** (already powers Goals: `ID,Name,Scope,Target,Saved,Per Month,…`) with a `Scope='Sinking'` value — **no new sheet tab**, and it rides the same read/write paths Goals already use. (b) A compact "🪣 Sinking Funds" section (inside Budget→Goals or its own card) listing each fund: name, target, saved-so-far, **suggested monthly set-aside** = `(target − saved) ÷ months until due`, and an on-track/behind chip (compare actual recent contributions vs the suggestion). (c) "Contribute" logs to `Allocation Transactions` under the fund's `Type` (same pattern Goals will use) so the money is real, not just a sheet number. (d) Dashboard surfaces the **total monthly set-aside across all funds** so it can be folded into the runway/forecast burn. Q1: Separate sinking-funds view, or merge into the Goals page? Q2: Should the suggested set-aside recompute every month as the deadline approaches (true amortization) or stay a flat figure you set once? Q3: Should sinking-fund set-asides count toward the Health-Score savings-rate signal? Q4: Pre-seed a few common funds (Car, Gifts, Insurance, Medical) or start empty? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 39 — Cash-Flow Low-Balance Forecast**: Runway (Task 35) and the Income Forecast (Task 16) answer "am I OK this month?" but not "will I dip below $0 on the 23rd before payday?" — the single most useful day-to-day question. PLAN: a forward **daily-balance projection** for the next 30–45 days that starts from current cash on hand and walks the calendar applying known future events: subscription due-dates (`Subscriptions` + existing `nextRenewal()`), recurring P1/P2 bill due-days (Task 23's `_fin_due_dates`), and expected paychecks (Task 20's `_fin_payday_config`). Renders a small line/area chart (Recharts, already imported) with a $0 (and configurable buffer) threshold line; **any day the projected balance crosses below the buffer is flagged** with "⚠ Tight around {date} — projected $X". Plain-English takeaway ("You're clear through payday" vs "You may run short ~3 days before payday — consider moving $Y"). Reuses already-loaded `Subscriptions`/`expenses`/`allAllocTx`; needs a "current cash on hand" anchor. Q1: Where does "current cash on hand" come from — sum of `Allocation Summary` balances, a single account balance you enter, or net of all allocations? Q2: Forecast window — 30, 45, or 60 days? Q3: Configurable low-balance buffer (e.g. warn below $100 not just $0)? Q4: Dashboard card or a panel beside the Payday tracker? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 40 — Spending Anomaly Detection**: Catch the charge that's wrong or out-of-character *before* it quietly blows the budget — a duplicate, a price hike, a mistyped amount, or an unusually large discretionary spend. PLAN: for each spend row in `allAllocTx` (already loaded), build a per-`Type` baseline from that category's trailing history (median + median-absolute-deviation, which is robust to outliers unlike mean/stdev), then **flag any new spend whose amount exceeds `median + k·MAD`** (k≈3) or is a near-duplicate (same Type + amount within a few days). Surface flags as a dismissable "🔎 N unusual charges this month" card (Dashboard or Transactions) listing each: category, amount, date, and why it's flagged ("3× your typical Groceries spend"). Dismissals remembered in `localStorage._fin_anomaly_seen` (opaque row hashes — no amounts). Purely read-only analysis; never edits or deletes a transaction.   - ✅ COMPLETED + VERIFIED (2026-06-06) — `AnomalyCard` component + pure `detectAnomalies(allAllocTx)` helper in Dashboard.jsx (right after `EmergencyFundCard`, before `export default`). - **Task 44 — Safe-to-Spend Today (unified daily number)**: The app already computes a per-day discretionary allowance, an income figure, upcoming bills (Tasks 16/23), and savings commitments — but nowhere collapses them into the one number people actually want each morning: *"how much can I spend today without breaking the month?"* PLAN: a prominent Dashboard hero chip "✅ Safe to spend today: $X" computed as **(money in this month − already-spent − still-owed fixed bills not yet funded − remaining savings target) ÷ days left in month**, all from already-loaded state (`income`/`spent` ground-truth totals, `expenses` allowances, `Subscriptions` due before month-end, savings-category allowances). Three-tier color (rose if ≤ $0, amber if running tight vs the full-month pace, teal if comfortable). Tap to expand the math: "money in $A − spent $B − unfunded bills $C − savings left $D = $E free ÷ N days." Reconciles with the existing "per-day flexible" figure (Dashboard.jsx `perDay`) but adds the bill/savings safety subtraction so it never tells you to spend money that's already promised. No new sheet tab; no new localStorage (pure derived view). Q1: Should "still-owed fixed bills" include ALL P1+P2 allowances not yet funded this month, or only subscription/dated bills due before month-end? Q2: Subtract the full remaining savings target, or treat savings as optional (don't subtract)? Q3: Hero chip at the very top of Dashboard, or fold it into the existing per-day allowance tile?   - ✅ COMPLETED + VERIFIED (2026-06-07) — `SafeToSpendCard({ income, spent, expenses, allAllocTx, daysLeftIncl, expanded, onToggle })` in Dashboard.jsx, defined immediately after `BudgetMixCard` (before `export default`). Plan defaults used: **Q1** reserve unpaid P1+P2 essentials (full allowance minus what's already spent on that line this month — so a paid bill isn't double-counted); **Q2** subtract the *unmet* remaining savings target (allowance − already-funded into that bucket this month); **Q3** a distinct collapsible card placed right after the Health-Score card / before the 6-Month Trend (kept separate from the existing discretionary "💸 Safe to spend / day" tile, which it complements); **Q4** a dimensionless tier — rose when `free ≤ 0`, amber when `< 15%` of remaining cash is free, teal otherwise. **Formula**: `free = (income − spent) − Σ max(0, essentialAllowance − spentOnThatType) − Σ max(0, savingsAllowance − fundedIntoThatBucket)`, then `perDay = max(0, free) / daysLeftIncl`. Essentials = the same P1+P2 non-Savings set `EmergencyFundCard`/`ForecastCard` reserve, so all three reconcile. Per-Type current-month sums are derived from `allAllocTx` (negatives → spent, positives → funded). Collapsed header shows the headline `$X/day` + "$free ÷ N days left"; expanded shows the full money-in − spent − bills − savings = free waterfall plus per-line "bills not yet covered" and "savings still to fund" breakdowns. Render-guarded by `expenses.length > 0 && income > 0` (hides on a fresh month until income is processed). **Read-only — zero new API calls, no new sheet tab, no new localStorage; build passes.**

- **Task 47 — Cash Envelope / Zero-Based "Every Dollar Assigned" Check**: The gold-standard budgeting discipline (YNAB / zero-based) is *give every dollar a job* — income minus all category allowances should equal exactly $0; a positive gap is unassigned money drifting toward impulse spends, a negative gap is an over-promised budget. The app already has the pieces (`income` ground-truth + `Monthly Expenses` allowances) but never surfaces the reconciliation. PLAN: a compact Dashboard "🧮 Every Dollar Assigned" card showing **assigned = Σ all `Monthly Allowance ($)`** vs **income this month**, with a single signed figure: *"$X left to assign"* (teal, prompts allocating it to savings/a goal) or *"$Y over-assigned"* (rose, your plan promises more than you earn). A thin 3-segment bar (essentials / wants / savings share of income, reusing Task 42's `buildMixMap` category mapping) visualises where the assigned dollars go, and a "to-zero" hint suggests the nearest savings bucket to park a surplus into. Tap to expand: per-tier assigned totals + the unassigned remainder. Reconciles with the Health-Score "allocation completeness" signal (both measure assigned-vs-income) so they never disagree. No new sheet tab; no new localStorage (pure derived view). Q1: Define "income" as this month's processed deposits (alloc ground-truth) or the recurring-income forecast average (so the target is stable month-to-month)? Q2: Should the card *only* appear when there's a non-trivial gap (e.g. |gap| > $20), or always show as a discipline tile? Execute? Y/N: **Y (built)**

- **Task 52 — Shared / Splittable Subscription Tracker**: Many subscriptions (family streaming plans, group software seats) are split with other people, so the *real* personal cost is a fraction of the billed `Amount` — but the budget counts the full charge, overstating subscription spend and the runway/forecast burn. Best practice is a periodic, consistent cadence so the trend line is real. PLAN: (a) **prompt for a fresh snapshot on month close** (and/or on the first Dashboard load of a new month) when the latest `Net Worth` snapshot is older than ~25 days — a one-tap "📈 Update your net worth for {Month}?" nudge that opens the existing `NetWorthModal` prefilled with last balances; never auto-writes without the user's tap (no silent duplicate-date rows). (b) **Growth insights** in the expanded card: month-over-month and annualised growth rate ("▲ 4.2%/mo · ~$X/yr at this pace"), plus a **savings-contribution attribution** that compares net-worth change to that month's net savings deposits so the user sees how much growth came from saving vs market/value change. (c) **Milestone push** (reuse Task 22 plumbing) when net worth crosses a round number ($10k, $25k, $50k, $100k…) — dedup in `localStorage._fin_nw_milestones`. Rides the existing `Net Worth` sheet tab + `_fin_networth_target`; new localStorage `_fin_nw_milestones` (array of crossed thresholds — integers only, no balances) + `_fin_nw_snap_prompted` (per-month dedup, date only). Q1: Prompt cadence — on month close, monthly regardless, or only when the last snapshot is >N days stale? Q2: Stale threshold — 25 days (plan), 30, or 45? Q3: Show the savings-vs-value-change attribution, or keep it to a simple growth %? Q4: Milestone thresholds — round $25k steps, or a custom list? Q5: Milestone push (Task 22 plumbing) + in-app, or in-app only? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 54 — Savings Account Interest / APY Yield Tracker**: Idle cash in a low-APY account is a silent, common money leak — the standard fix is to know each savings bucket's APY and what it's actually earning. The app tracks balances (Net Worth, Allocation Summary) but has no concept of yield. PLAN: store an optional APY per cash/savings account in the existing `Net Worth` **Notes** column as a compact tag (`apy:4.5`) — **no schema change** — parsed client-side. A "💵 Interest & Yield" panel (in the Net Worth expanded card or Summary→Year) then shows, per account: balance × APY = projected annual interest, a blended portfolio APY, and a **leak flag** when a large balance sits in a sub-1% account ("$X earning ~0% — at 4.5% that'd be ~$Y/yr"). A plain "your cash is on track to earn ~$Z this year" headline. Read-only analysis over already-loaded Net Worth rows; the only write is the APY tag the user sets via a small field in `NetWorthModal`. No new sheet tab; nothing newly sensitive (APY %, not balances, is the only new datum and it lives in the sheet). Q1: Store APY in the Net Worth Notes tag (plan) or add an `APY` column? Q2: Flag idle cash below a threshold APY (e.g. <1%) and against what benchmark (a fixed 4.5%, or a figure you set)? Q3: Panel inside the Net Worth card, or a section in Summary→Year? Q4: Only savings/cash account types, or any asset with an APY tag? Q5: Should projected interest feed the Net Worth growth attribution (Task 53)? Execute? Y/N:
- **Task 55 — Financial Independence (FI) / Coast-FIRE Progress**: The headline long-horizon metric serious personal-finance practice tracks is *how close am I to never needing to work* — `FI number ≈ annual essential spending × 25` (the 4% rule), and Coast-FIRE (the amount that, left to compound, reaches FI by a target age without further contributions). The app already has both inputs: net worth (Task 14) and annual essential burn (Task 35's P1+P2 × 12). PLAN: a collapsible "🔥 Financial Independence" card showing **FI number = essentialBurn×12×25**, **% to FI = netWorth ÷ FInumber**, a progress bar, and a plain-English "at your recent savings rate you'll reach FI in ~N years" projection (using the 6-month income/savings average already computed for the Forecast/Health cards). Optional **Coast-FIRE** line — "you're already coast-FI for age 60" once net worth × (1.07^yearsToTarget) ≥ FInumber. A configurable withdrawal rate (default 4%) and target age in `localStorage._fin_fire_config`. Read-only over already-loaded net worth + burn + savings-rate state. No new sheet tab; new localStorage `_fin_fire_config` ({rate, targetAge} — no balances). Q1: Withdrawal rate — fixed 4% (plan) or configurable (3.5%/4%/5%)? Q2: Essential burn basis — P1+P2 only (true FI floor, plan) or include P3 (comfortable FI)? Q3: Show the Coast-FIRE line too, or keep it to the FI number + % only? Q4: Expected real return for the projection — 5%, 7%, or configurable? Q5: Dashboard card or a panel in Summary→Year? Execute? Y/N:

- **Task 57 — Category Spend-Pace / End-of-Month Burn-Down Projection**: Budgets are judged at month-end, but the useful question mid-month is *"at my current pace, will this category blow its budget?"* The app shows actual-vs-allowance today but never projects the finish. PLAN: for each `Monthly Expenses` category, take this month's actual spend so far (Σ `allAllocTx` negatives by `Type`, already loaded) and **project end-of-month spend = actual ÷ fraction-of-month-elapsed** (linear run-rate, the standard burn-down estimate), then compare to the allowance. A "📉 Spend Pace" panel (Budget→Categories header, or a Dashboard card) flags categories **projected to exceed budget** ("Groceries: $180 spent on day 12 → ~$465 projected vs $400 budget — trim ~$65") and shows an overall "on pace to spend $X vs $Y budgeted this month." Y/N: **Y (built 2026-06-22 — picked as the safest read-only high-value task since no Drive approvals were pending)**
  - ✅ COMPLETED + VERIFIED + DOUBLE-CHECKED (2026-06-23) — `SpendPaceCard` + pure `computeSpendPace(expenses, allAllocTx, dayOfMonth, daysInMo)` in `Dashboard.jsx` (right after `AnomalyCard`, before `BudgetMixCard`). Plan defaults: **linear run-rate** `projected = spent ÷ (dayOfMonth/daysInMo)` (Q1); **flag `over > $0.50`** = projected-over by any meaningful amount (Q2); **Dashboard card** (Q3); **spendable categories only** — `Expense !== 'Savings'` & allowance > 0, and only categories with `spent > 0` this month so zero-spend lines don't add noise (Q4); **suppressed in the first 2 days** via the `dayOfMonth >= 3` render guard (Q5). Current-month spend per `Type` = Σ abs of negative `allAllocTx` rows whose `dateStr.slice(0,7)` matches the current `YYYY-MM`. Collapsed: "N categories on pace to overspend" (amber) / "On pace — every category within budget" (emerald) + "projected $X vs $Y budgeted" (with "$Z over" when total projected > total budgeted). Expanded: flagged rows (or top-6 by `over` when none flagged), each a **pace bar** — fill = `min(100, spent/allow×100)` coloured amber when over / emerald when on-pace, plus an absolutely-positioned vertical marker at `dayOfMonth/daysInMo×100`% (month-elapsed); a fill past the marker means spending faster than the calendar — with a "trim ~$over" / "on pace for ~$projected" line. - **Task 58 — Financial-Ratios Panel (Debt-to-Income, Debt-to-Asset, Liquidity)**: Net Worth (Task 14) gives the headline number, but lenders and personal-finance best practice judge health by *ratios* — the app has every input (net worth assets/liabilities + monthly income + essential burn) and never surfaces them. - **Task 63 — Variable-Income Smoothing Buffer ("pay yourself a steady amount")**: With art commissions + business income, real monthly income is lumpy — the budgeting best practice for irregular earners is to pool surplus in fat months and draw a *steady* "salary to self" in lean ones, so the budget isn't whiplashed by income swings. - **Task 65 — Quarterly Estimated-Tax (1040-ES) Tracker & Reminders**: Task 15 now estimates your annual net SE income and a 25–30% set-aside, but self-employed filers actually owe taxes *quarterly* (Form 1040-ES) — and missing a quarter triggers IRS underpayment penalties. ### New Tasks 68–70 (best-practice expansions proposed 2026-06-21, building on the new Debt Payoff Tracker) — awaiting Execute Y/N
- **Task 68 — Log Debt Payment → Budget + Net-Worth Sync**: The Debt card (Task 26) projects payoff and snapshots balances, but a payment still has to be *recorded by hand* in two places — the budget (so cash-out is tracked) and the next debt snapshot (so the balance drops). PLAN: a **"💵 Log payment"** action on each debt row that, in one tap, (a) appends an `Allocation Transactions` spend row `[today, "Debt: {name}", −amount, "Debt payment", 'Debt', true]` so the money shows in budget history (mirrors Task 9's goal-contribution write); (b) writes a fresh debt snapshot with that debt's balance reduced by the principal portion (`amount − thisMonth's interest`), so the payoff projection and pay-down % advance immediately; and (c) re-pulls so the Debt card, the trend line, and the milestone check all reconcile. An optional "this was extra (above minimum)" flag feeds the avalanche/snowball roll-over. Because debt principal reduces what you owe, the same payment also nudges Net Worth up the next time it's snapshotted. Reuses the existing `appendRow`/`saveDebts` plumbing; no new sheet tab. Q1: Should a logged payment auto-write a new debt snapshot (plan), or just log the cash-out and let me update balances manually? Q2: Split the payment into interest vs principal automatically (using the stored APR), or treat the whole amount as principal for simplicity? Q3: Tag the budget row's Account as `'Debt'` (a new bucket) or an existing account you pick? Q4: Should logging a payment that clears a debt to $0 fire a "paid off {name}! 🎉" push? - **Task 69 — Debt-Free Date Countdown & Interest-Cost Awareness Card**: The Debt card shows payoff time only when expanded; the single most motivating number for someone in debt is a always-visible **"debt-free on {Month YYYY} — N months to go"** countdown, plus the often-shocking **total interest you're on track to pay**. Collapsed header shows the countdown when `chosen.paidOff && months>0` and the interest clock when `monthInterest>0.5`; expanded shows the +$50 nudge (or the get-on-track variant via `boost.paidOff` when minimums don't cover interest).   - ✅ COMPLETED + VERIFIED (2026-06-24) — built entirely in `ProcessIncome.jsx` by folding manual overrides into the **single `deposits` memo** that already feeds tier totals, account tiles, the surplus calc, the success count, and the sheet write — so one hand-edit flows through the whole modal *and* the log (the user's "make sure it's reflected in the rest of the log" ask) with a minimal, low-risk surface. **Plan-answer defaults:** edit the **dollar amount** per category (Q1); **always start from the auto-suggestion** — no saved named templates in v1 (Q2, deferred); **allow committing an under/over split with a colour-coded warning** rather than blocking (Q3); **keep priority/proportional as the editable seed** (Q4); **surplus rows stay on the existing weighted-bucket logic** — manual category edits simply change how much surplus remains, which the weighted buckets then absorb (Q5). **Mechanics:** new state `manualMode` (off by default → pure auto-split, zero behaviour change) + `overrides = { [type]: editedAmountString }`. `baseDeposits` = `calcDeposits(...)` (unchanged); the new `deposits` memo returns `baseDeposits` verbatim unless `manualMode`, in which case each row whose `type` has a non-empty override gets `deposit = max(0, parseFloat(override))` with recomputed `coverage`/`pct`. **UI:** (a) an "✏️ Adjust amounts manually" toggle + "↻ Reset to auto" (clears `overrides`) below the coverage line; (b) a live tally banner — `{fmt(totalDeposited)} of {fmt(amount)} assigned` with `leftToAssign = amount − totalDeposited` shown as emerald "✓ fully assigned" (|gap|<$0.01), amber "$X left to assign" (under), or rose "$X over" (over); (c) in the per-account category rows, the static `+{fmt(d.deposit)}` becomes a `$`-prefixed number `<input>` (seeded with the auto figure, `onFocus` selects, writes to `overrides[type]`). `handleProcess` is **unchanged** — it still appends one row per `d.deposit > 0`, now reading the overridden amounts. **Deferred (documented, not built):** the optional `_fin_alloc_manual_last` "use my usual split" ratio memory (Q2) and editing categories with a $0 sheet allowance (only the auto-eligible set is editable in v1). **Build passes (`npm run build` clean).** See the **"## Manual Allocation Override (Task 77)"** doc block below.

- **Task 127 — Robust income basis (median / trimmed-mean) for lumpy art + commission income**: With art commissions + business income the monthly income series is *lumpy* — one big commission month inflates the last-6 **mean**, so the Forecast/Every-Dollar "typical income" overstates a normal month. The standard fix for skewed data (already used by the anomaly detector, Task 40, via median+MAD) is a **median or trimmed mean** (drop the single highest and lowest month), which is robust to one-off spikes. Q1: Offer mean / median / trimmed (plan), or just switch the default to median? Q2: Trimmed = drop 1 high + 1 low (plan) or a percentage? ### Build summary (latest run, 2026-06-20)
**Task 15 (Tax Prep Summary) is COMPLETED — it was the highest-effort approved-but-unbuilt task.** Built a read-only **🧾 Tax Prep sub-view inside the Summary→Year tab** (sibling of Task 11's 📊 Year-to-Date view via a `yearSub` pill toggle — no new nav item, respecting the user's standing nav-clutter concern). The new `TaxView` + module helpers (`IS_OWNER_DRAW_TX`, `IS_BIZ_DEDUCT_SUB`, `extractSource`, `txMonthly`, `yearOf`) live in `Summary.jsx`. It produces a **Schedule C estimate** — `revenue` (Σ `Business Transactions` col F) − `COGS` − `OpEx` − deductible subscriptions = **estimated net self-employment income** — with COGS/OpEx split *identically* to the Business `InsightsView` P&L (`cat==='COGS'`→COGS, else OpEx, owner draws excluded) so the two screens reconcile; a **25–30% tax set-aside** suggestion; a year picker (current + 2 prior); and an informational **personal-income-by-`[Source]`-tag** breakdown (Task 27-ready, clearly marked non-deductible). Deductible subscriptions are detected from the `Subscriptions` Notes column (`/business|deduct/i`) and annualised. **Export:** "📋 Copy summary" → plaintext via clipboard with a textarea fallback (Task 31 pattern). ## Monthly Statement (Task 31) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-04
- Two builders in Dashboard.jsx, both inside the component (closure access to `monthNote`, `healthScore`, `pm`, `MONTHS`):
  - `printStatement(current, stmtTxns, expenses, currentMonth, currentYear)` — opens a print window, `document.write(html)`, auto-`print()` after 600ms. All sheet-sourced strings go through `esc()` before injection (XSS guard for `document.write`).
  - `copyStatementText(...)` — same data, plain-text output, `navigator.clipboard.writeText` with a hidden-textarea `execCommand` fallback. Sets `stmtCopied` (2s).
- Statement month note read fresh from `_fin_month_notes[`${year}-${MONTHS.indexOf(month)+1}`]` (NOT the `monthNote` state) so it's correct for closed months too.
- Top Expenses = top-5 of `catMap` where `spend>0` (negative rows only — income/deposits never appear here); share % = `spend / totalSpent`.
- UI buttons live in the Monthly Statement modal sticky header (`showStatement`), only when `!stmtLoading && !stmtError`: "📋 Copy text" (slate) then "🖨 Save PDF" (blue).
- Print CSS: `@page letter`, `@media print { print-color-adjust: exact }`, `.note-callout` amber left-rule.

- `SpendingCalendarCard` reducer (Dashboard.jsx ~199): `amount>0 → income`, else `→ spend (abs)`. `spendColor()` colors rose ONLY when `spend>0`; a pure-income day (`spend===0 && income>0`) returns teal `bg-teal-800/60`. The corner teal dot shows only when a day has BOTH income and spend. ⇒ an income row can never paint a day rose. Verified by trace; build passes.

## Emergency Fund / Runway Tracker (Task 35) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-05 · DOUBLE-CHECKED 2026-06-21 · 2026-07-07
- **DOUBLE-CHECK (2026-07-07): VERIFIED** — re-traced `EmergencyFundCard` (Dashboard.jsx ~741, chosen as an independent money-calc not checked in ~2 weeks): `burn` = Σ `pm('Monthly Allowance ($)')` over `burnItems` = expenses with `Priority ∈ {1,2}` (default `'3'` via `?? '3'`), `Expense !== 'Savings'`, allowance > 0; `savings` = Σ over `bucketBal` = per-`type` net signed `allAllocTx.amount` for types in the `Expense==='Savings'` set (deposits + / spends −); `return null` when `burn <= 0`; `runway = savings/burn`; tiers red `<1` / amber `<3` / teal else; `pct = max(0, min(1, runway/target))`; `shortfall = max(0, burn*target − savings)`; `pickTarget` writes `_fin_ef_target` and `getEFTarget` guards to 1/3/6 (default 3). Matches the documented spec exactly; independent of this run's Task-143 edit; `npm run build` passes. No further double-check needed.
- **DOUBLE-CHECK (2026-06-21): VERIFIED** — re-traced `EmergencyFundCard` (Dashboard.jsx ~564): `burn` = Σ P1+P2 non-Savings `Monthly Allowance ($)`; `savings` = net signed allocations summed over the `Expense==='Savings'` Type set; `runway = savings/burn`; tiers rose `<1` / amber `1–3` / teal `≥3`; `pct = min(1, runway/target)`; `shortfall = max(0, burn*target − savings)`; `return null` when `burn <= 0`; 1/3/6 target picker writes `_fin_ef_target`. Matches spec exactly; build passes. No further double-check needed.
- Component `EmergencyFundCard({ expenses, allAllocTx, expanded, onToggle })` in Dashboard.jsx, defined immediately after `ForecastCard` (before `export default function Dashboard`).
- **Burn** = Σ `pm(e['Monthly Allowance ($)'])` for `expenses` where Priority ∈ {1,2} and `Expense !== 'Savings'` — same essential set as `ForecastCard`'s `recurringAllow`, so the two cards reconcile.
- **Savings on hand** = for each `allAllocTx` row whose `type` is in the set of `expenses` Types with `Expense === 'Savings'`, sum the signed `amount` (deposits + / spends −). Total across buckets = savings.
- **Runway** = `savings / burn` (months). Tiers: rose `<1`, amber `1–3`, teal `≥3`. `return null` when `burn <= 0`.
- Target cushion: module helper `getEFTarget()` reads localStorage `_fin_ef_target` (allowed values 1/3/6, default 3 — integer count only, no financial data). In-card 1/3/6 picker calls `pickTarget(n)` which sets state + writes localStorage.
- Collapsed header: "X.X months covered" + progress bar (`pct = min(1, runway/target)`) + shortfall line (`max(0, burn*target − savings)`). Expanded: savings/burn tiles, target picker, P1+P2 burn breakdown (sorted desc), per-bucket savings balances.
- State `efExpanded` in Dashboard; rendered after `ForecastCard`, before `SpendingCalendarCard`, guarded by `expenses.length > 0 && allAllocTx.length > 0`. Zero new API calls, no new sheet tab.

## Spending Anomaly Detection (Task 40) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-06
- Pure helper `detectAnomalies(allAllocTx)` + component `AnomalyCard({ allAllocTx, expanded, onToggle })` in Dashboard.jsx, defined immediately after `EmergencyFundCard` (before `export default`). Module helpers: `median(arr)`, `getAnomalySeen()`. Consts `ANOMALY_K=3`, `ANOMALY_MIN_HISTORY=5`, `ANOMALY_KEY='_fin_anomaly_seen'`.
- **Inputs**: only spend rows (`amount < 0`), recorded as positive magnitudes; bucketed `byType`. "Current month" = rows whose `dateStr.slice(0,7)` === `YYYY-MM` of today.
- **Size flag**: baseline = that Type's prior-month spends; needs `≥ ANOMALY_MIN_HISTORY`. `med=median(amts)`; `scaled=1.4826*median(|a−med|)` with floor `scaled = max(scaled, med*0.10)`; `threshold = med + 3*scaled`. Flag when `amount > threshold && amount >= med*1.5`. Reason = `${(amount/med).toFixed(1)}× your typical {Type} spend`.
- **Duplicate flag**: O(m²) over current-month spends; same Type + `|Δamount|<=0.01` + `|Δdays|<=3` → the later-dated row flagged "Possible duplicate". `flagged` Set prevents double-listing a hash already flagged as size.
- **Hash** = `Type|dateStr|amount.toFixed(2)`. Dismiss ✕ appends to `_fin_anomaly_seen` (array, capped `slice(-200)`) — opaque keys only, no standalone $ amounts. Flags filtered against `seen`; `return null` when `flags.length === 0` (card hidden when clean).
- Newest-first sort by `dateStr`. Read-only — never writes/edits/deletes a transaction. State `anomalyExpanded` in Dashboard; rendered after `EmergencyFundCard`, before `SpendingCalendarCard`, guarded by `allAllocTx.length > 0`. Zero new API calls, no new sheet tab.

## Budget Balance — Savings-Rate Trend & 50/30/20 (Task 42) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-07
- Pure helpers `buildMixMap(expenses)` + `computeBudgetMix(allAllocTx, expenses)` + `mixMonthLabel(key)` + component `MixSparkline({values})` + `BudgetMixCard({ allAllocTx, expenses, expanded, onToggle })` in Dashboard.jsx, defined immediately after `AnomalyCard` (before `export default`). Consts `MIX_TARGET={needs:50,wants:30,savings:20}`, `MIX_COLORS` (needs `#0ea5e9` sky / wants `#f59e0b` amber / savings `#10b981` emerald).
- **`buildMixMap`**: `Type`(lowercased) → `'needs'|'wants'|'savings'`. Savings always wins (`Expense==='Savings'`); else Essentials/Stability→needs, Discretionary/Subscription→wants; else Priority fallback (`'1'|'2'`→needs, else wants).
- **`computeBudgetMix`**: buckets each *positive* `allAllocTx` deposit by `YYYY-MM` and category (unmapped Type → `wants`); income basis = that month's total deposits so `needsPct+wantsPct+savingsPct === 100`. Returns last-6 months chronological with `$` + `%` per bucket. `.filter(total>0).slice(-6)`.
- **Card**: `return null` when no months. Collapsed = latest-month "X% needs · Y% wants · Z% savings" + a single 3-segment split bar. Expanded = green/amber target chips (grace ±1pt: needs ≤51, wants ≤31, savings ≥19), 6-month stacked `BarChart` with `stackOffset="expand"` + two `ReferenceLine`s at `y=0.50` and `y=0.80` (fractions because expand normalises 0..1), savings-rate figure + `MixSparkline` (inline SVG, target dashed line at 20%) + "▲/▼ N pts over M mo", plain-English takeaway.
- `ReferenceLine` added to the existing `recharts` import (already a dep — no new package). State `mixExpanded` in Dashboard; rendered after `AnomalyCard`, before `SpendingCalendarCard`, guarded by `allAllocTx.length > 0 && expenses.length > 0`. **Read-only — zero new API calls, no new sheet tab, no new localStorage.**

## Safe-to-Spend Today (Task 44) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-07 · DOUBLE-CHECKED 2026-06-24 · 2026-07-04
- **DOUBLE-CHECK (2026-07-04): VERIFIED** — re-traced `SafeToSpendCard` (Dashboard.jsx ~1247): `curKey = YYYY-MM`; `spentByType`/`fundedByType` bucket current-month `allAllocTx` (negatives→spent abs, positives→funded); `owedEssentials` = Σ over P1+P2 non-Savings allowance>0 of `max(0, allow − paid)`; `unmetSavings` = Σ over `Expense==='Savings'` allowance>0 of `max(0, allow − saved)`; `net = income − spent`; `free = net − owedEssentials − unmetSavings`; `perDay = daysLeftIncl>0 ? max(0,free)/daysLeftIncl : 0`; `tightRatio = net>0 ? free/net : (free>0?1:0)`; tiers red (`free≤0`) / amber (`<0.15`) / teal — all match the documented spec exactly. Confirmed this run's Task-125 edit (in the *separate* EveryDollarCard) does not touch this card. Build passes. No further double-check needed.
- **DOUBLE-CHECK (2026-06-24): VERIFIED** — re-traced `SafeToSpendCard` (Dashboard.jsx ~1147): current-month per-Type sums from `allAllocTx` (`dateStr.slice(0,7)===curKey`; negatives→`spentByType` abs, positives→`fundedByType`); `owedEssentials` = Σ `max(0, allowance − paid)` over P1+P2 non-Savings; `unmetSavings` = Σ `max(0, allowance − funded)` over `Expense==='Savings'`; `net = income − spent`; `free = net − owedEssentials − unmetSavings`; `perDay = daysLeftIncl>0 ? max(0,free)/daysLeftIncl : 0`; tiers rose (`free≤0`) / amber (`free/net<0.15`) / teal — all match the documented spec exactly. It is a self-contained `rounded-2xl p-4 border` block with no fixed width, so it renders correctly as a cell in the new Task 71a insight grid and expands only its own cell (`items-start`). Build passes. No further double-check needed.
- Component `SafeToSpendCard({ income, spent, expenses, allAllocTx, daysLeftIncl, expanded, onToggle })` in Dashboard.jsx, defined immediately after `BudgetMixCard` (before `export default function Dashboard`).
- **One unified daily number** distinct from the existing discretionary "💸 Safe to spend / day" tile (which is `flexLeft ÷ daysLeftIncl`). This card answers "what can I spend without breaking the month" after reserving bills + savings.
- **Formula**: `net = income − spent`; `free = net − owedEssentials − unmetSavings`; `perDay = max(0, free) / daysLeftIncl`.
  - `owedEssentials` = Σ over P1+P2 non-Savings `expenses` of `max(0, Monthly Allowance ($) − spentOnThatType_thisMonth)` — only the UNPAID portion, so an already-paid bill isn't double-counted. (Same essential set `EmergencyFundCard`/`ForecastCard` reserve → all three reconcile.)
  - `unmetSavings` = Σ over `Expense==='Savings'` items of `max(0, allowance − fundedIntoThatBucket_thisMonth)`.
  - Per-Type current-month sums come from `allAllocTx` filtered to `dateStr.slice(0,7) === YYYY-MM`: negatives → `spentByType` (abs), positives → `fundedByType`.
- **Tiers** (dimensionless, works at any income): `free ≤ 0` → rose ("everything's spoken for, hold off"); `free/net < 0.15` → amber (tight); else teal.
- Collapsed = headline `$X/day` + "$free ÷ N days left". Expanded = full waterfall (money in − spent − bills owed − savings to set aside = free) + per-line "Bills not yet covered" and "Savings still to fund" lists.
- State `safeExpanded` in Dashboard; rendered **after HealthScoreCard, before TrendChartCard**, guarded by `expenses.length > 0 && income > 0` (hides on a fresh month until income is processed). `income`/`spent` are the Dashboard's existing ground-truth current-month totals. **Read-only — zero new API calls, no new sheet tab, no new localStorage.**

## Debt Payoff Tracker (Task 26) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-21
- **Task 69 add-on (2026-06-23):** the collapsed header carries a "🏁 Debt-free {Mon YYYY} · N to go" countdown + "⏱ interest accruing this month" clock, and the expanded Result box a "+$50/mo saves X mo / $Y interest" nudge — all via `debtFreeLabel(months)` (after `fmtMonths`) + `monthInterest`/`boost`/`monthsSaved`/`interestSaved50` in the `DebtCard` body, pure read-only over `simulatePayoff`. See the Task 69 entry in the drafted-tasks list above for the full reference.
- **A Dashboard card** (mirrors Net Worth — chosen over a standalone page because the user flagged the bottom nav is getting busy). New **`Debts` sheet tab** `Date | Name | Type | Balance | APR | MinPayment | Notes`. Like Net Worth, **a snapshot = all of one date's rows**; "Update balances" appends one row per debt stamped today, so total debt plots a pay-down trend. All balances live in the private sheet; only an opaque list of crossed milestone thresholds (`_fin_debt_milestones`, ints) is on-device.
- **Module-level (in Dashboard.jsx, right after `NetWorthCard`, before the Top-Goal widget):**
  - `getDebtMilestones()` — reads `_fin_debt_milestones` (array-guarded).
  - `buildDebtSnapshots(rows)` — groups by ISO `date` → `[{date, items, total, minTotal}]` ascending (`total`=Σ balance, `minTotal`=Σ minPayment).
  - `orderDebts(items, strategy)` — `snowball` → ascending balance; else (`avalanche`) → descending APR.
  - `simulatePayoff(items, strategy, extra)` — month-by-month: each remaining debt accrues `bal*(apr/100/12)` interest, then a **constant** `monthlyPay = Σ minimums + max(0,extra)` is applied — minimums first (in priority order), surplus (extra + minimums freed by cleared debts = roll-over) thrown at the highest-priority remaining debt. Filters cleared debts each month so `monthlyPay` stays constant (roll-over). Returns `{months, totalInterest, paidOff}`; `CAP=1200` months guards a payment too small to cover interest (`paidOff=false`).
  - `fireDebtMilestones(paidPct)` — fires a deduped browser push at 25/50/75/100% pay-down (vs **peak** snapshotted total); no-ops when `Notification` undefined/denied; `requestPermission` when not yet granted.
  - `fmtMonths(m)` — "X yr Y mo".
  - `DebtCard({ rows, expanded, onToggle, onUpdate })` — empty state = slim dashed CTA. Local state `strategy` ('avalanche'|'snowball'), `extra` (0–1000 slider). `peak` = max total across snapshots; `paidPct = (peak−latestTotal)/peak`; `useEffect(()=>fireDebtMilestones(paidPct), [paidPct])`. Header: total owed (rose), debt count, `minTotal`/mo, MoM delta (▼ = emerald). Expanded: strategy toggle + explanation, extra-payment slider, `simulatePayoff` result (debt-free in `fmtMonths`, total interest, total/mo) or a "minimums don't cover interest" warning when `!paidOff`, the avalanche-vs-snowball interest-saved line, per-debt list in payoff order (numbered, APR, balance), a `ComposedChart` `<Line>` total-debt trend (rose, reuses already-imported recharts), and a pay-down `ProgressBar` vs peak.
- **Dashboard body:**
  - States: `debtRows`, `debtExpanded`, `showDebt`, `debtSaving`, `debtError`.
  - Load: `readRange(token, 'Debts!A:G', 'UNFORMATTED_VALUE').catch(()=>[])` added to the main `Promise.all` (8th entry; destructured as `debtSheetRows`); parsed (skip a `Date`/`Name` header row) → `{date: nwDateToIso, name, type, balance: pm, apr: pm, minPayment: pm, notes}`. Re-pulls on `refreshKey` bump.
  - `saveDebts(debts)` — `ensureSheetTab('Debts')` → ensure header row → append one row per debt stamped today → `setRefreshKey(k=>k+1)`. (Mirrors `saveNetWorth`.)
  - `<DebtCard>` rendered **after `NetWorthCard`, before `AnomalyCard`** (always rendered — empty state is the dashed CTA).
  - `DebtModal` (inline, next to `NetWorthModal`): seeds rows from the last snapshot or a Credit-Card default; per-row name/balance/APR/min inputs; live total-owed + min/mo tally; "Save snapshot" → `saveDebts` (filters to rows with a name and balance>0).
- **Plan-answer defaults:** Dashboard card (not standalone page) · avalanche/snowball interest-difference shown · debt type = free-text label · "Log Payment" cross-write deferred → **Task 68**.

## Net Worth Snapshot (Task 14) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-12
- **The one feature here that WRITES to the sheet** (unlike the other read-only Dashboard cards). New `Net Worth` sheet tab, columns `Date | Account | Type | Balance | Notes`. All balances live in the private sheet; the only on-device storage is the optional target int (`_fin_networth_target`).
- **Module-level (before `export default`, right before the Dashboard component):**
  - `getNWTarget()` — reads `_fin_networth_target`, returns null when unset/≤0.
  - `nwDateToIso(raw)` — normalises a serial number / `YYYY-MM-DD` / `M/D/YYYY` to ISO `YYYY-MM-DD` (so snapshots sort/group regardless of sheet locale; ISO strings sort lexicographically).
  - `nwIsLiability(type)` — `String(type).toLowerCase().startsWith('l')`.
  - `buildNetWorthSnapshots(rows)` — groups parsed rows by ISO `date` → `[{date, items, assets, liab, net}]` sorted ascending. `assets`=Σ non-liability balances, `liab`=Σ liability balances, `net = assets − liab`.
  - `nwLabel(iso)` — "Mon D" display label.
  - `NetWorthCard({ rows, expanded, onToggle, onUpdate })` — empty state = slim dashed CTA (mirrors payday-setup); otherwise headline net worth (emerald ≥0 / rose <0) + MoM delta vs the previous snapshot. Expanded: Assets/Liabilities tiles, a `ComposedChart` `<Line>` trend over snapshots (uses already-imported recharts; **no LineChart import needed** — ComposedChart hosts the Line), optional target `ReferenceLine` + progress bar, per-account breakdown (liabilities shown `−$X`), and the **📊 Update balances** button.
- **Dashboard body:**
  - States: `netWorthRows`, `nwExpanded`, `showNetWorth`, `nwSaving`, `nwError`.
  - Load: `readRange(token, 'Net Worth!A:E', 'UNFORMATTED_VALUE').catch(() => [])` added to the main `Promise.all`; parsed (skip leading `Date` header row) → `{date: nwDateToIso, account, type, balance: pm, notes}`. Re-pulls on `refreshKey` bump.
  - `saveNetWorth(accounts)` — `ensureSheetTab` → ensure header row → append one row per account stamped `today` (ISO), then `setRefreshKey(k=>k+1)`. **A snapshot = all of one date's rows.**
  - `<NetWorthCard>` rendered in the cards stack **after `EmergencyFundCard`, before `AnomalyCard`** (always rendered — empty state is the dashed CTA, so it's discoverable).
  - Update modal: inline `NetWorthModal` next to `PaydayConfigModal`. Seeds rows from the last snapshot (prefilled balances) or Checking/Savings/Credit-Card defaults; Asset/Owe toggle per row; live Assets/Owe/Net tally; optional "Target net worth" field (writes `_fin_networth_target`); "Save snapshot" calls `saveNetWorth`.
- **Defaults chosen (plan Qs):** user-defined free-text accounts · Dashboard card (not standalone page) · liabilities entered positive, app negates · optional target marker · manual snapshot only (no auto-snapshot on month close → avoids duplicate-date snapshots).

## Tax Prep Summary (Task 15) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-20
- **All in `Summary.jsx`. READ-ONLY — zero sheet writes, no new sheet tab, no new localStorage.** Lives as a sub-view of the existing **Year tab** (toggle `yearSub` ∈ {`'ytd'`,`'tax'`}; default `'ytd'`), so Task 11's YTD view and this Tax view share one tab and neither adds a nav item (the user's recurring nav-clutter concern).
- **Module helpers (right after `YearView`, before `TABS`):** `IS_OWNER_DRAW_TX(d)` = `String(d).toLowerCase().includes('processed as personal income')` (same owner-draw detector as Business `InsightsView`, so COGS/OpEx reconcile); `IS_BIZ_DEDUCT_SUB(n)` = `/business|deduct/i.test(n)`; `extractSource(desc)` = `/^\[([^\]]+)\]/` → the `[Source]` tag (Task 27-ready) or null; `txMonthly(amount, cycle)` = subscription billed→monthly run-rate (mirrors Dashboard `toMonthly`); `yearOf(raw)` = `parseAllocDate(raw)?.getFullYear()` (handles serial + string dates).
- **`TaxView({ bizTx, bizExp, bizSpend, subs, allocRows, year, onYear, availableYears, loading })`** — one `useMemo` computes everything for `Number(year)`:
  - **Schedule C revenue** = Σ `Business Transactions` col F (index 5) for rows whose `yearOf(col A) === Y` (skips a leading `Date` header).
  - **Cost rows** = `Business Expenses` (`{cat:col D, amount:col C}`, needs both) + non-owner-draw `Business Account Spending` (`{cat:col B, amount:col C}`, `!IS_OWNER_DRAW_TX(col E)`), each year-filtered. `COGS` = Σ `cat === 'COGS'`; `OpEx` = Σ everything else, with `opexByCat` breakdown (sorted desc) — identical split to the Business P&L.
  - **Deductible subscriptions** = `subs` (skip header) where `IS_BIZ_DEDUCT_SUB(Notes col E)`, each annualised `txMonthly(Amount, Cycle)×12` (current run-rate — no per-year subscription history); `subDeduction` = Σ.
  - **`netSE = revenue − COGS − OpEx − subDeduction`**; set-aside = `max(0,netSE) × {0.25, 0.30}`.
  - **Personal income** (informational, NOT deductible) = positive `allocRows` (col C `pm > 0`) for the year, bucketed by `extractSource(col D)` (untagged → "Untagged income"), sorted desc + total.
  - **Export** `buildText()` → plaintext; `copyText()` → `navigator.clipboard.writeText` with hidden-textarea `execCommand` fallback (Task 31 pattern); "📋 Copy summary" flips to "✓ Copied" 2s.
  - UI: year picker (current + 2 prior), amber "Estimate only — not tax advice" caveat banner, Schedule C waterfall (OpEx + subs expandable), indigo set-aside card, expandable personal-income card, mileage note (no fabricated figure).
- **Main component wiring:** states `yearSub`,`taxYear`,`taxBizTx`,`taxBizExp`,`taxBizSpend`,`taxSubs`,`taxLoaded`,`taxLoading`. Lazy-load effect fires only when `tab==='year' && yearSub==='tax' && !taxLoaded` — `Promise.allSettled` over `Business Transactions!A:H`, `Business Expenses!A:G`, `Business Account Spending!A:E` (all UNFORMATTED), `Subscriptions!A:E`. Personal side reuses the Year tab's `yearAllocRows`. Render: Year tab shows the ytd/tax pill toggle, then `<YearView>` or `<TaxView>`; the tile-grid + legend stay guarded by `tab !== 'year'`.
- **Plan-answer defaults:** calendar-year basis + year picker (Q1) · mileage NOT auto-included, shown as a note (Q2) · 25–30% set-aside range (Q3) · COGS=cat 'COGS', else OpEx (Q4) · business-only deductions, personal informational (Q5).

## Quick-Log from Category Card (Tasks 99 + 101 + 102 + 108 + 111) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-29 · DOUBLE-CHECKED 2026-06-30
- **Magnitude-scaled ladder (Task 111):** module helper `stepLadder(magnitude)` (after `pushQuickLogRecent`) → `{steps, round}` by the category's `Monthly Allowance`: `>$500` → `[25,100,250,500]`/round-$25 · `$50–$500` → `[5,20,50,100]`/round-$5 · `<$50` → `[1,5,10,20]`/round-$1 (also the default when `magnitude` is 0/absent). `QuickLogDrawer` takes an optional `magnitude` prop → `ladder = useMemo(stepLadder(magnitude), [magnitude])`; the stepper row renders `ladder.steps.map` and round-up = `Math.ceil(c/ladder.round)*ladder.round`. Threaded `magnitude={allowance}` (`itemGoal(item)`) from `BudgetCard`, `magnitude={budgeted}` from `CategoryItemCard`. Kind-independent (magnitude only). Pure local-state; no new write/tab/storage/API.
- **DOUBLE-CHECK (2026-06-30 #2): Task 102 VERIFIED** — re-traced the recents path (it shares the drawer Task 108 edited): `getQuickLogRecent(type)` returns `[]` for no type, parses `_fin_quicklog_recent`, `Array.isArray`-guards `all[type]`, filters to `{a:number>0}`; `pushQuickLogRecent(type, amount, kind)` guards `type && amount>0`, object-guards the parsed map, `a = parseFloat(amount.toFixed(2))`, dedups `[{a,k:kind}, ...prev.filter(r => !(r.k===kind && |r.a−a|<0.005))].slice(0,3)`, try/catch-silent write. Chip row renders only when `recents.length>0`; tap does `setAmount(r.a.toFixed(2)); setKind(r.k==='fund'?'fund':'spend')` (no auto-save); `save()` calls `pushQuickLogRecent(type, val, kind)` with the positive magnitude `val` after the successful append, so the just-logged amount becomes next time's top chip. The Task-108 stepper row sits *below* the amount input (recents row is *above* it) — no conflict; both only `setAmount`. Build passes. No further double-check needed.
- **Amount steppers / round-up (Task 108):** in `QuickLogDrawer`, a chip row directly under the amount input — `+$1/+$5/+$10/+$20` add to the current value (`setAmount(v => (Math.max(0,(parseFloat(v)||0)+n)).toFixed(2))`), **⤴ Round up** = `Math.ceil` to next dollar, **✕ Clear** (shown only when an amount is entered) = `setAmount('')`. Pure local-state; commit path untouched; no storage/API.

## Manual Allocation Override (Task 77) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-24
- **All in `src/components/ProcessIncome.jsx`.** Lets the user hand-steer each category's deposit instead of accepting the priority/proportional auto-split. **No new sheet tab, no new localStorage in v1; the sheet write path is unchanged.**
- **Key design:** overrides fold into the **single `deposits` memo** (the one thing that feeds `tierTotals`, `byAccount`, `accountTiles`, `depositPlan`, `surplus`/`totalDeposited`, the success-count, and `handleProcess`). So a manual edit propagates everywhere — including the logged rows — with no ripple edits elsewhere.
- **State (declared right before the `deposits` memo):** `manualMode` (bool, default `false`) · `overrides` (`{ [type]: editedAmountString }`, default `{}`).
- **Memos:** `baseDeposits = useMemo(calcDeposits(...))` (the old `deposits`, untouched). New `deposits = useMemo(...)`: returns `baseDeposits` verbatim unless `manualMode`; then per row, if `overrides[d.type]` is a non-empty string → `deposit = Math.max(0, parseFloat(ov)||0)`, `coverage = allowance>0 ? (already+dep)/allowance : 0`, `pct = amount>0 ? dep/amount : 0`. Rows the user hasn't touched keep their auto figure.
- **Tally:** `leftToAssign = amount − totalDeposited` (signed; defined next to `surplus`). Banner: emerald "✓ fully assigned" when `|leftToAssign| < 0.01`, amber "$X left to assign" when `>0`, rose "$X over" when `<0`. **Under/over is allowed** (commit never blocked) — surplus auto-absorbs a positive remainder via the existing weighted buckets.
- **UI:** (a) toggle "✏️ Adjust amounts manually" + "↻ Reset to auto" (`setOverrides({})`, shown only when overrides exist) inserted right after the "Monthly goal / % covered" line in the Inputs section, gated `amount > 0 && !histLoading`. (b) The tally banner below it. (c) In the per-account category render loop, the static `+{fmt(d.deposit)}` becomes (when `manualMode`) a `$`-prefixed `<input type=number>` whose value is `overrides[d.type] ?? d.deposit.toFixed(2)`, `onFocus` selects all, `onChange` writes `overrides[d.type]`. `CoverageChip` stays beneath it.
- **`handleProcess` is unchanged** — still appends one `Allocation Transactions` row per `d.deposit > 0` using the (now possibly overridden) `deposits`.
- **Plan-answer defaults:** dollars per category (Q1) · always seed from auto, no saved named splits yet (Q2 → drafted as Task 80) · allow under/over commit with colour warning (Q3) · priority/proportional as the seed (Q4) · surplus stays on the weighted-bucket logic (Q5).
- **v1 limits (documented):** only the auto-eligible rows (allowance>0 or live-gas) are editable — $0-allowance / ad-hoc buckets are drafted as **Task 81**; percentage-input mode is drafted as **Task 82**.

## Gas Coverage (Task 72) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-25
- **All in `src/pages/Summary.jsx`. READ-ONLY — zero sheet writes, no new sheet tab.** Answers the user's "is my gas budget enough?" request with a clear verdict, reusing the gas figures the Summary already computes (`c.gasPerGal`, `c.mpg`, `c.claimableGas`, `c.dim`).
- **Module-level (right before `renderTile`):** `GAS_MILES_KEY='_fin_gas_miles'`, `getGasMiles()` (parses the stored monthly-miles count, returns null when unset/≤0), and `GasCoverageTile({ c })`.
- **`GasCoverageTile`** holds local state `miles` (init from `getGasMiles()`), `editing`, `draft`. `defaultMiles = round(GAS_MILES_PER_DAY × dim)` (56.6 mi/day × days-in-month — the same assumption the `budgetFor2QC` tile uses, so they reconcile); `monthlyMiles = usingDefault ? defaultMiles : miles`. `return null` when `c.gasPerGal ≤ 0` (no price → can't judge).
- **Formula:** `gallonsNeeded = monthlyMiles ÷ mpg`; `needed = gallonsNeeded × $/gal`; `gallonsBuys = claimableGas ÷ $/gal`; `milesCovers = gallonsBuys × mpg`; `coverage = claimableGas − needed`. `enough = coverage ≥ 0`.
  - **Enough** (emerald card): "✅ Enough — covers ~{milesCovers} mi" + "Your {claimable} gas budget buys ~{gallonsBuys} gal at {$/gal}/gal — enough for your ~{monthlyMiles} mi/mo."
  - **Short** (amber card): "⚠ Short ~{|coverage|}/mo" + "Your ~{monthlyMiles} mi/mo needs ~{gallonsNeeded} gal ≈ {needed}; you have {claimable}. Add {|coverage|} to this month's gas budget."
- **Editable miles:** "✏ miles" toggles an inline number input → `saveMiles()` writes `localStorage._fin_gas_miles`; `resetMiles()` removes it (back to the 56.6 mi/day default). Footer line states whether it's using the default assumption or the user's figure.
- **Wiring:** `gasCoverage` added to `renderTile` switch (returns `<GasCoverageTile c={c} />`), to `DEFAULT_ORDER.gas` after `claimableGas`, and to `WIDE_TILES`. Import adds `GAS_MILES_PER_DAY` from `../lib/gasBudget`.
- **Robustness:** `activeOrder` now appends any `DEFAULT_ORDER[tab]` ids missing from the user's saved per-tab order (`summary_order_<tab>`), so a newly-added tile shows even for users who've dragged-to-reorder that tab.
- **Plan-answer defaults:** Q1 user-entered monthly miles (default 56.6/day) · Q2 Summary gas tile (GasPrices.jsx mirror → Task 84) · Q3 advisory only, no auto-write (one-tap allowance write → Task 83) · Q4 live EIA `c.gasPerGal` · Q5 `c.mpg` from Expense Summary.

## Section Alert Auto-Expand (Task 90) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-28
- **All in `src/pages/Dashboard.jsx`. Read-only / state-only — no sheet writes, no new API calls, no new sheet tab, no new localStorage.** Closes the gap the Task-86 collapsible sections introduced: a folded section could hide a fresh warning. Now an alert force-opens its section (once per session) and badges the header.
- **`InsightSection({ title, open, onToggle, badge = 0, children })`** — gained a `badge` prop; when `>0` renders a right-aligned amber pill "⚠ {badge}" (`ml-auto … text-amber-300 bg-amber-500/15 border-amber-500/30 rounded-full`). Header grid otherwise unchanged.
- **State + effect (right after `toggleInsightSection`, in the hooks region BEFORE the `loading`/`error` early returns):** `const [sectionAlerts, setSectionAlerts] = useState({spending:0, saving:0})` + `const sectionAutoOpened = useRef({})`. One `useEffect(..., [expenses, allAllocTx])`:
  - **spendingN** = `detectAnomalies(allAllocTx).filter(f => !getAnomalySeen().includes(f.hash)).length` + `(dom >= 3 ? computeSpendPace(expenses, allAllocTx, dom, dim).flagged.length : 0)` where `dom`/`dim` are computed locally from `new Date()` (so the effect doesn't depend on the post-early-return `dayOfMonth`/`daysInMo`).
  - **savingN** = `1` when EF `burn > 0 && savings/burn < 1`, else `0` — `burn` = Σ P1+P2 non-Savings `Monthly Allowance ($)`, `savings` = Σ net allocations into `Expense==='Savings'` Type buckets (mirrors `EmergencyFundCard` exactly so they reconcile).
  - `setSectionAlerts({spending: spendingN, saving: savingN})`, then `setInsightSections(prev => …)` force-opens any folded section that now has an alert **without persisting** (saved collapse preference intact), guarded by `sectionAutoOpened.current[key]` → fires once per session. The user can re-collapse via `toggleInsightSection` (which DOES persist), and on the next load the alert re-opens it. No infinite loop: effect deps are `[expenses, allAllocTx]` only.
- **Wiring:** `badge={sectionAlerts.spending}` on 💵 Spending & Pace, `badge={sectionAlerts.saving}` on 🏦 Saving & Net Worth; the Task-78a "Insights" bar shows an aggregate "⚠ {spending+saving}" pill (Q5) so a warning is visible even when all sections are folded.
- **Plan-answer defaults:** Q1 Anomaly + Spend-Pace + EF-runway-<1mo · Q2 force-open every load while alert persists, once per session · Q3 "⚠ N" badge on header · Q4 still user-collapsible for the session (force is in-memory only) · Q5 aggregate badge on the Insights bar too.

## Section-level Fold-All / Show-All (Task 95) — COMPLETED + VERIFIED 2026-06-28 #2
- **All in `src/pages/Dashboard.jsx`. Pure state — no sheet writes, no new API calls, no new sheet tab, no new localStorage** (reuses `_fin_insight_sections`). Completes the density arc (71a grid → 78a card-collapse-all → 86 sections → 88a per-card persistence → 90 alerts): the most compact "just show me the headers" view took a tap per section; now it's one tap.
- **Helper (right after `toggleInsightSection`):** `anySectionOpen = spending || saving || planning`; `setAllSections(open)` writes `{spending,saving,planning} = open` to state + `_fin_insight_sections` in one shot.
- **Insights bar (Task-78a header) now hosts two controls in a `flex gap-3` on the right:** (1) the existing **card collapse-all** (`⊟ Collapse all`/`⊞ Expand all` → `setAllInsightCards`), **rendered only when `anySectionOpen`** — folded sections hide their cards, so the card control would be a no-op then; (2) the new **section fold-all** (`⊟ Fold sections`/`⊞ Show sections` → `setAllSections(!anySectionOpen)`).
- **Composes with Task 90:** the section-alert auto-open fires once per session via `sectionAutoOpened.current`, so folding sections after it has fired won't be force-overridden — but the `⚠ N` header badge (Task 90) persists regardless of fold state, so a live warning is never buried even in the headers-only view.
- **Plan-answer defaults:** Q1 two separate controls (sections vs card bodies — clearer than a magic combined tap), card control hidden when all sections folded · Q2 persist to `_fin_insight_sections` · Q3 Task-90 badge keeps alerts visible when folded (safety) · Q4 labels "⊟ Fold sections"/"⊞ Show sections" · Q5 on the existing Insights bar.

## Git Workflow
1. Source changes → main branch directly (no PRs per user preference)
2. Deploy: `npm run deploy` on `main` → builds dist/ → pushes to `gh-pages`

## Security Checklist
- [ ] No API keys or tokens in source code or commit history
- [ ] No financial data (amounts, sheet contents) in GitHub
- [ ] All user data stays in their private Google Sheet
- [ ] Google OAuth scope is `spreadsheets` only (not drive, gmail, etc.)
- [ ] PIN prevents unauthorized access if device is shared
